         <div style="clear:right">

         <div class="t">
          If I were to even see someone famous I would be so shocked that they could be in the middle of murdering someone or having sex or something and I'd be like "Hey, you're (whoever it is)!" without even thinking about it. I'd like to think I'd be cool about it but realistically I've never met anyone famous so especially if it's someone from something I like I would be crazy excited and probably make a fool of myself.
         </div>
